#############SS Unit creation###########
####Fascist Militia#######

	country_event = {
		id = 48902

		trigger = {
			ideology_group = fascism
			not = { has_country_flag =  fascist_militia_brigade_activation }	
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_fascist_militia_brigade_activation }				
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 1
		}	
		
		title = "Fascist Militia Brigade"
		desc = "EVTDESC48902"
		picture = "EVT91129"
		
		option = {
			name = "Activate This Unit"
			set_country_flag = fascist_militia_brigade_activation
			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		}
		
		option = {
			name="No need"
			set_country_flag = no_fascist_militia_brigade_activation
			clr_country_flag = fascist_militia_brigade_activation
			ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		}
	}
############SS Infantry#############
	country_event = {
		id = 48903
		
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			has_country_flag =  fascist_militia_brigade_activation
			has_country_flag = SS_Waffen_creation
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_infantry_brigade_activation }	
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_ss_infantry_brigade_activation }				
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 6
		}	
		
		title = "SS Infantry Brigade"
		desc = "EVTDESC48903"
		picture = "ssinf"
		
		option = {
			name = "Activate This Unit"
			set_country_flag = ss_mixed_support_brigade_activation
			set_country_flag = ss_infantry_brigade_activation
			set_country_flag = ss_support_activation
			ai_chance = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		option = {
			name="No need"
			set_country_flag = no_ss_infantry_brigade_activation
			ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		}
	}

####  SS-Panzer-Generalkommando Creation  ####
##############################################
country_event = {
		id = 94063
		
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			or = {
				date = 1942.6.1
				has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical
			}
			controls = 1861 # Berlin
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_panzer_creation }
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 1
		}
		
		title = "EVTNAME94063"
		desc = "EVTDESC94063"
		picture = "EVT94050"
		
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA94063"
			supplies = -2500 #Equipment needed
			manpower = -5
			set_country_flag = SS_panzer_creation
			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

            OMG = {
                any_country = {

		light_armor_brigade_design = 1

		not = { has_country_flag =  ss_light_armor_brigade_activation }

		not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}	
	
	title = "SS leicht Panzer Brigade"

	picture = "kampfgruppen"
	
	option = {
		name = "Activate This Unit"

	}
	
	option = {
		name="No need"

	}

country_event = {
		id = 49298
		
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical }
			controls = 1861 # Berlin
			OR = {
				POL = { government_in_exile = yes }
				NOT = { exists = POL }
				controls = 1928 # warsaw
				has_country_flag = fr_goal_nag
			}
			has_country_flag = Heimwehr_Danzig
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_Heimwehr_Danzig_disbanded}
			not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 1
		}
		
		title = "SS Heimwehr Danzig Disbands"
		desc = "This unit will become part of the Totenkopf Division"
		picture = "ss-disbanded-unit-Heimwehr-Danzig"
		
		option = {
			name = "Gut"
			remove_brigade = "SS Heimwehr Danzig"
			remove_brigade = "SS Wachsturmbann Eimann"
			manpower = 10
			supplies = 500
			set_country_flag = SS_Heimwehr_Danzig_disbanded
			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		}
	}

			not = { has_country_flag =  no_SS }
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 2
		}
		
		title = "EVTNAME94022"
		desc = "EVTDESC94022"
		picture = "Schutzen_Staffel"
		
		option = {
			name = "Historical Division Upgrades"
			supplies = -2500 #Equipment needed
			manpower = -30
			officer_pool = -1000
			set_country_flag = zDD_SS_starting_oob
			set_country_flag = ss_starting
			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		}
		option = {
			name = "Ahistorical Full Divisions"
			set_country_flag = ss_ahistorical
			ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		}
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB94022"
			set_country_flag = no_SS			
			ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		}
	}

		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			or = {
			year = 1945
			surrender_progress = 80 }
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical }
			controls = 1861 # Berlin
			controls = 1910 # Amsterdam
			controls = 2198 # Eindhoven	
			controls = 1742 # Stettin
			supplies = 1500
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_ned_net }

		}

			name = "OK"
			supplies = -1000 #Equipment needed
			set_country_flag = SS_ned_net
			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

            OMG = {
                any_country = {
                    limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        total_ic = 10
                        not = { total_ic = 200 }
                    }
                    add_country_modifier = {
                        name = "15IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_V"
                        duration = 110
                    }

                }

country_event = {

			war = yes
			has_country_flag = foreign_SS_units_decision
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_karst_ita }
			or = {
				and = {
					year = 1944
					month = 9
					ITA = { faction = axis }
				}
				and = {
					exists = RSI

		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {

#### Italy										####
#### 29. Waffen.Gren.Div. der SS (ital.Nr.1)	####

country_event = {
		id = 94024
		
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			controls = 1861 # Berlin
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical }
			3694 = { controller = { faction = axis } } # Cremona
			has_country_flag = foreign_SS_units_decision
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_italnr1_ita }
			or = {
				and = {
					year = 1945
					month = 1
					ITA = { faction = axis }
					#not = { ita_lybia = { controlled_by = ITA } }
				}
				and = {
					exists = RSI
					RSI = { faction = axis }
				}
				and = {
					year = 1943
					#ita_rsi44 = { controlled_by = GER }
					not = { war_with = ITA }
					not = { war_with = RSI }

		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			year = 1944
			month = 10
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical }
			controls = 1861 # Berlin
			controls = 2890 # Zwettl
			has_country_flag = foreign_SS_units_decision
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_rum_rom }
			war_with = SOV
			ROM = { faction = axis }
				
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 1
		}
		
		title = "EVTNAME94035"
		desc = "EVTDESC94035"
		picture = "EVT94035"
		
		option = {
			name = "OK"
			supplies = -100 # Equipment needed
			load_oob = GER/zDD-SS-Rumanis_Nr_1.txt
			set_country_flag = SS_rum_rom
			ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
		}
		
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA94000"
			manpower = 1
			set_country_flag = SS_rum_rom
			ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
	}

#### 38. SS-Grenadier-Division 'Nibelungen'	####

country_event = {
		id = 94049
		
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			or = {
			year = 1945
			surrender_progress = 80 }
			not = { has_country_flag =  ss_ahistorical }
			controls = 1861 #Berlin
			controls = 3155 #Rosenheim
			or = {
			   GER = { lost_national = 10 }
			   and = {
				   #not = { num_in_faction = 4 }
					BUL = { not = { faction = axis } }
					ROM = { not = { faction = axis } }
					ITA = { not = { faction = axis } }
					FIN = { not = { faction = axis } }
					2041 = { not = { controlled_by = GER } }	#Warsaw
					2678 = { not = { controlled_by = GER } } #Paris
				}
			}
			or = {
				war_with = USA
				war_with = ENG
				war_with = SOV
			}
			not = { has_country_flag = SS_38_gren }
			has_country_flag = SS_Waffen_creation
		}
		
		mean_time_to_happen = {
			days = 1
		}
		
		title = "EVTNAME94049"
		desc = "EVTDESC94049"
		picture = "EVT94049"
		
		option = {
			name = "OK"
			set_country_flag = SS_38_gren
			ai_chance = { factor = 99 }

            OMG = {
                any_country = {
                    limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        total_ic = 10
                        not = { total_ic = 200 }
                    }
                    add_country_modifier = {
                        name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_III"
                        duration = 90
                    }	
                    load_oob = GER/zDD-SS-Grenadier-Division.txt
                }
            }
            OMG = {
                any_country = {
                    limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        total_ic = 200
                        not = { total_ic = 250 }
                    }
                    add_country_modifier = {
